2. through "get info" i changed the permissions to "read & write" on
everything (except public) for htdocs/wordpress and all the contained
folders. did not work.
3. i downloaded filezilla to change the permissions, but i can't connect to
the server because i don't know the host or the username/password.

Most sites say just put your domain, but i haven't connected my domain to
wordpress yet. Plus i'm just trying to change the wordpress permissions,
but it's located in my htdocs folder, which (i assume) is the folder who's
permission i have to change.
